<analysis>
The previous AI engineer initiated the project by comprehensively reviewing the existing codebase to understand its scope, technology stack, and functionality. A critical early discovery was the discrepancy between the system's stated FastAPI/Python backend and the actual Laravel/PHP implementation. The engineer meticulously explored both backend (Laravel controllers, models, routes) and frontend (React components, pages, services). After generating an initial project scope report, the engineer faced challenges with the PHP environment (missing  and  binaries), which was eventually resolved by a backend testing sub-agent. The primary task then shifted to removing hardcoded data, which involved creating new backend API endpoints, models, migrations, and corresponding frontend services and context providers. Subsequently, the engineer created extensive documentation. The work paused while the engineer began restructuring project files, after a brief misinterpretation of the user's request. A notable discrepancy was the engineer's assertion that the frontend was working beautifully despite explicit screenshot tool errors. The project is currently a functional Laravel/React application, with an ongoing effort to rationalize the codebase structure and consistency.
</analysis>

<product_requirements>
The user tasked the AI engineer with taking over an existing MVP-level Mewayz application, aiming to expand and modify its functionality. The core problem is enhancing a full-stack application (React frontend, Laravel PHP backend, with MariaDB and MongoDB integration). The application is described as having a professional UI, with key features including Authentication, Workspace Management, Social Media tools, Payments, Email Marketing, CRM, Courses, and Products.

Explicit user requests and their current status:
1.  **Project Scope Documentation:** Create a detailed rapport ( file) outlining the project's current scope, functionality (backend/frontend), and technical details. This was successfully completed with  and  documents, detailing the Laravel 12 + React 18 + MariaDB stack.
2.  **Hardcoded Data Removal:** Identify and replace all hardcoded data with dynamic data fetched from the database. This involved significant backend (new controllers, models, API routes, migrations) and frontend (new services, , component updates) modifications. This task is largely complete but may have lingering linting issues.
3.  **Tech Stack Consistency:** Ensure no duplicated tech stacks exist, specifically indicating Flutter should be reserved only for mobile native development. The engineer performed a cleanup of potentially duplicated frontend service files (, ) and updated relevant implementations.
4.  **Documentation Update:** Create and update all relevant documentation files reflecting the current accurate state of the project. This resulted in a comprehensive suite of updated documentation (API, developer, database, deployment, security, user, feature guides).
5.  **Project Restructuring:** Merge, change, and remove files to make the overall project structure more professional and consistent. This task is currently in progress.
</product_requirements>

<key_technical_concepts>
-   **Full-Stack Development**: React.js (frontend) and Laravel (PHP backend).
-   **Database**: MariaDB (primary, used by Laravel), MongoDB (mentioned in system prompt, but its actual usage with Laravel is unclear from trajectory).
-   **UI/UX**: Tailwind CSS, Framer Motion.
-   **Authentication**: Laravel Sanctum with JWT tokens.
-   **Package Management**: Composer (PHP), Yarn (Node.js).
-   **Process Management**: Supervisor.
-   **API Design**: Backend API routes prefixed with .
</key_technical_concepts>

Core components like , , , and  were updated to consume data via these new services and contexts, eliminating hardcoded values. Linting errors were frequently reported during these file writes.
